if (!is_file('.idea/php.xml')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: .idea/php.xml');
	writefile_1();
	if (!is_file('.idea/php.xml')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): .idea/php.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('.idea/php.xml') != '09cf0a9f30eb27bf8a48da582b8d8d450efe4aac') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): .idea/php.xml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('.idea/php.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of .idea/php.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('.idea/php.xml') !== '09cf0a9f30eb27bf8a48da582b8d8d450efe4aac') {
		if (@sha1_file('.idea/php.xml') !== '36609362f317573125074570a12ec42881b8245b') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: .idea/php.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('.idea/php.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('.idea/php.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('.idea/php.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('.idea/php.xml') !== '09cf0a9f30eb27bf8a48da582b8d8d450efe4aac') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): .idea/php.xml');
		}
	}
}

	@fclose($fp);
}
if (!is_file('.idea/trunk.iml')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: .idea/trunk.iml');
	writefile_2();
	if (!is_file('.idea/trunk.iml')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): .idea/trunk.iml');
	} else if (sha1_file('.idea/trunk.iml') != 'a6673695fc1b8fde8b759d0c571b5bc027cfddeb') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): .idea/trunk.iml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('.idea/trunk.iml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of .idea/trunk.iml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('.idea/trunk.iml') !== 'a6673695fc1b8fde8b759d0c571b5bc027cfddeb') {
		if (@sha1_file('.idea/trunk.iml') !== 'f70b98c6d2b1b6b05d87b2ac85d1ba28a36d182e') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: .idea/trunk.iml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('.idea/trunk.iml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('.idea/trunk.iml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('.idea/trunk.iml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('.idea/trunk.iml') !== 'a6673695fc1b8fde8b759d0c571b5bc027cfddeb') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): .idea/trunk.iml');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('dev/test_logmasks')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: dev/test_logmasks');
	writefile_14();
	if (!is_file('dev/test_logmasks')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): dev/test_logmasks');
	} else if (sha1_file('dev/test_logmasks') != '30e700867af679fc223290cb3c7bae71a5aaf942') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): dev/test_logmasks');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('dev/test_logmasks', 0755)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of dev/test_logmasks');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('dev/test_logmasks') !== '30e700867af679fc223290cb3c7bae71a5aaf942') {
		if (@sha1_file('dev/test_logmasks') !== '0d10c865e5e95317bd9b265415ec67ca8eac9d49') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: dev/test_logmasks');
			$tmp = pathinfo('dev/test_logmasks');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('dev/test_logmasks')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('dev/test_logmasks', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_14();
		if (@sha1_file('dev/test_logmasks') !== '30e700867af679fc223290cb3c7bae71a5aaf942') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): dev/test_logmasks');
		}
	}
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps');
	writefile_15();
	if (!is_file('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps');
	} else if (sha1_file('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps') != 'f9833f163640b4dcb081814b82f76bd271713113') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps', 0755)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps') !== 'f9833f163640b4dcb081814b82f76bd271713113') {
		if (@sha1_file('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps') !== 'abf1c43b0075d03936c7e4a2d4fb891c2f22b8ac') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps');
			$tmp = pathinfo('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_15();
		if (@sha1_file('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps') !== 'f9833f163640b4dcb081814b82f76bd271713113') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps');
		}
	}

if (!is_file('includes/functions.inc.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/functions.inc.php');
	writefile_17();
	if (!is_file('includes/functions.inc.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/functions.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/functions.inc.php') != '4179010ac435fca58e9b30793ebccd9aeafd393f') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/functions.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/functions.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/functions.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/functions.inc.php') !== '4179010ac435fca58e9b30793ebccd9aeafd393f') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/functions.inc.php') !== '5d6d038c98bc0448d41ed36d48d240f5f32488aa') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/functions.inc.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/functions.inc.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/functions.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/functions.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_17();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/functions.inc.php') !== '4179010ac435fca58e9b30793ebccd9aeafd393f') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/functions.inc.php');
		}
	}
}
